cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// semaphore ID, 0x0-0x7, to SMPH_ID. The request is sticky and once the
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is asserted. This event is deasserted when SW
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// releases the semaphore or a new ID is written to SMPH_ID.
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// Note: SW must wait until SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is triggered before
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// writing a new ID to SMPH_ID . Failing to do so might lead to permanently
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_W                                          3
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_M                                 0x00000007
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_S                                          0
cpu/abc.txt:cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#endif // __AUX_SMPH__

cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// semaphore ID, 0x0-0x7, to SMPH_ID. The request is sticky and once the
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is asserted. This event is deasserted when SW
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// releases the semaphore or a new ID is written to SMPH_ID.
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// Note: SW must wait until SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is triggered before
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// writing a new ID to SMPH_ID . Failing to do so might lead to permanently
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_W                                          3
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_M                                 0x00000007
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_S                                          0
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc13xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#endif // __AUX_SMPH__

cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// Field:   [2:0] SMPH_ID
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// semaphore ID, 0x0-0x7, to SMPH_ID. The request is sticky and once the
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is asserted. This event is deasserted when SW
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// releases the semaphore or a new ID is written to SMPH_ID.
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// Note: SW must wait until SMPH_AUTOTAKE_DONE event is triggered before
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:// writing a new ID to SMPH_ID . Failing to do so might lead to permanently
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_W                                          3
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_M                                 0x00000007
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#define AUX_SMPH_AUTOTAKE_SMPH_ID_S                                          0
cpu/cc26xx-cc13xx/lib/cc26xxware/inc/hw_aux_smph.h:#endif // __AUX_SMPH__
